class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span <span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:NameControllingParty\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\" tupleRef=\"_I1126276426\" order=\"1\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Songbird\n Estates plc</span></ix:nonNumeric></span>.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><div><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns1:DescriptionPrincipalActivities\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA; mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;&#xD;&#xA; mso-highlight:white\">The principal activity of the company is to act as a\n construction and design manager for building projects in Canary Wharf and\n various other sites in London. </span><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA; &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p></ix:nonNumeric></div><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">BUSINESS REVIEW</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">In November 2008, J.P.\nMorgan appointed the company to act as development and construction<a></a> manager of the site at Riverside South, under a contract with a\nterm to October 2016. The<a></a> contract includes a right of first\noffer in the event J.P. Morgan decides to sell the site.<a></a> J.P.\nMorgan instructed the company to proceed with certain infrastructure works,<a></a> consisting of river wall protection, utilities installation and\nthe lower ground level floor slabs. These works are now substantially completed\nand J.P.Morgan has agreed that the riverside walkway should be reopened until\nthe next stage of construction commences.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The company received 76.0\nmillion as an advance of developer's profit in conjunction with<a></a>\nthe development. This sum will be set against the company's entitlement to\nfuture profits if J.P. Morgan proceeds with full construction.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The company is acting as\nConstruction Manager for the development at 20 Fenchurch Street, a<a></a> 50:50 joint venture between the Group and Land Securities Group\nplc. Planning consent for a<a></a> 37 storey building was granted in\nOctober 2009. The building will provide approximately<a></a> 690,000\nsq ft of world class space in floor plate sizes of 14,000 sq ft to 28,000 sq\nft,<a></a> with a sky garden on the top 3 floors. Construction\ncommenced on site in January 2011 and<a></a> is progressing on\nschedule and within budget. The building has been topped out and the cladding\nis substantially completed. The development achieved practical completion for\ntenant fit out in March 2014.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">In July 2011, the Group\nand Qatari Diar Real Estate Investment Company concluded an<a></a>\nagreement to redevelop the Shell Centre. The company will act as construction\nmanager for<a></a> the project. The development will be mixed use,\ncomprising office, residential and retail<a></a> space which will\nregenerate an important section of the South Bank in central London. The<a></a> joint venture parties submitted a planning application for 1.4\nmillion sq ft (net) in<a></a> December 2012 and planning consent was\nawarded in May 2013 subject to the Greater London<a></a> Authority\nand Secretary of State approval. In September 2013, the joint venture was\nnotified that the Secretary of State had called in planning application. The\nplanning<a></a> inquiry concluded in December 2013 and on 6 June\n2014 it was announced that the Secretary of State had given the green light to\nthe redevelopment.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;&#xD;&#xA;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:&#xD;&#xA;AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection4\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Construction\ncommenced on the Crossrail station at Canary Wharf in May 2009 and has<a></a> progressed ahead of schedule. The platform level was handed\nover to Cross London Rail Links<a></a> Limited in March 2012,to\nenable access for the tunnelling machines. The tunnel boring<a></a>\nmachines have passed through the station and the platform levels handed back to\nthe Group<a></a> for the next phase of works. The project is\nperforming well against budget. The first trains are due to run in 2018 when\nCrossrail opens for passenger service. The structure is complete and internal\nworks are well advanced.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Construction is\nprogressing well on 115,000 sq ft of retail and leisure accommodation above<a></a> the Crossrail station, of which 100,000 sq ft is retail. Within\nthe development, 96,000 sq ft is scheduled to open for trade in May 2015, ahead\nof the actual station opening in 2018.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Construction of the 44,000\nsq ft expansion of Jubilee Place mall completed and the mall opened for trade\non 1 November 2013.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As well as the retail\nexpansion projects referred to above, work continued on 25 Churchill<a></a> Place, a new office building of over 500,000 sq ft. Work on the\nbuilding began in February<a></a> 2012 and the structure was\nformally topped out in February 2013. Cladding and building<a></a>\nservices are complete and undergoing testing. Construction is on schedule for\ndelivery in<a></a> mid 2014.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As shown in the company's\nprofit and loss account, the company's profit after tax for the<a></a>\nyear was 6,390,959 (2012: 3,796,740). </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The balance sheet shows\nthe company's financial position at the year end and indicates that<a></a> net assets were 11,393,534 (2012: 7,292,575). Details of\namounts owed to group companies are shown in Note 11. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The Canary Wharf Group\n(comprising Canary Wharf Group plc and its subsidiaries) manages its<a></a> operations on a unified basis.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>For this reason, the company's directors believe that key<a></a>\nperformance indicators specific to the company are not necessary or appropriate\nfor an<a></a> understanding of the development, performance or\nposition of its business.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The\nperformance<a></a> of the Canary Wharf Group, which includes style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">As a member of the Canary\nWharf Group the key risks facing the company include<a></a> the\ncyclical nature of the property market, financing risk and concentration risk.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Cyclical Nature of the\nProperty Market</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The core construction\nbusiness of the company is subject to many external economic and<a></a>\nmarket factors. Following the turmoil in the financial markets and uncertainty\nin the Eurozone of recent years the property and construction markets had to\ncope with a decline in demand and a potential oversupply of office space. The\npossible oversupply of available space in the market was, however, mitigated by\nthe difficulty in securing finance for speculative development leading to\nreduced supply. The market was assisted by the continuing presence of overseas\ninvestors attracted by the relative transparency of the real estate market in\nLondon which is still viewed as both stable and secure. The market has also\nbeen underpinned by continuing demand for sites capable of incorporating\nresidential development. In the latter half of 2013, there was strong evidence\nof increasing demand for office space and a related increase in confidence in\nthe office real estate market. Changes in financial, property and construction\nmarkets are kept under constant review so that the company can react\nappropriately and tailor its business accordingly.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Financing Risk</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The broader economic cycle\ninevitably leads to movements in inflation, interest rates and<a></a>\nbond yields. The company finances its operations largely through surplus cash\nand intercompany finance. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The majority of Canary\nWharf Group's real estate assets, including the assets of the<a></a>\ncompany, are currently located on or adjacent to the Canary Wharf Estate with a\nmajority of<a></a> tenants linked to the financial services\nindustry.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Wherever possible steps are\ntaken to<a></a> mitigate or avoid material consequences arising\nfrom this concentration and to diversify<a></a> the tenant base.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" an<a></a> equal working environment where all employees\nare treated with respect and dignity.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The<a></a> company continues to keep employees informed of\nevents relevant to their employment via<a></a> 'all staff'\ncommunications and an intranet. Staff consultative committees, at which matters<a></a> raised by employees are considered by management and staff\nrepresentatives, have been established and meet every two months. The company's\nemployment policy is regularly reviewed to incorporate changes to legislation\nand ensure best practice is maintained.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Training and development</span></b><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The key to the company's\nsuccess is the people that work for the company.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The company<a></a> recognises the\nneed to continuously invest in the training of its workforce to ensure the<a></a> future success of the company. Commitment to training and\ndevelopment is given to all<a></a> individuals and the annual\nappraisal process plays a key role in facilitating managers and<a></a>\nemployees to identify training and development requirements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This information is used to<a></a>\nformulate the training programme for the following year using both formal and\non the job<a></a> training methods.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The performance appraisal process also promotes regular discussions and\nfeedback on how an individual's performance can improve, identify development\nneeds and opportunities for career progression. The company operates a graduate\nscheme.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The company is committed\nto ensuring, as far as is reasonably practicable, the health,<a></a>\nsafety and wellbeing of its employees, tenants and visitors and of all those\naffected by<a></a> its undertakings.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The company's framework for the management of\nhealth and safety is the<a></a> internationally recognised standard\nOHSAS 18001.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This standard is externally\nverified via a system of continuous assessment and audit and further supported\nby the formally adopted Group health, safety and welfare policy.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The company strives for\ncontinuous improvement to ensure a safe and healthy environment is<a></a> maintained and adequate resources are made available for these\npurposes.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The Group's<a></a>\nhealth and safety departments are committed to supporting all employees in\nunderstanding<a></a> their health and safety responsibilities\nthrough a system of processes and procedures in order to deliver the safest\nstandards within the built environment.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" acceptable at any level.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The company has adopted a formal anti bribery\nand<a></a> corruption policy which requires all directors and\nemployees to act in a manner to ensure<a></a> that the objectives\nof the policy are achieved.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The company\nhas a strict approach to maintaining high standards of finance, business\nprinciples and ethics.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" operations.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New state of\n affairs of the company and of the profit or loss of the company for that\n period.<a></a> In preparing these financial statements, the\n directors are required to:</span></p><p style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">Scope of the audit of the\nfinancial statements</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">An audit involves\nobtaining evidence about the amounts and disclosures in the financial<a></a> statements sufficient to give reasonable assurance that the\nfinancial statements are free<a></a> from material misstatement,\nwhether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This\nincludes an assessment<a></a> of: whether the accounting policies\nare appropriate to the company's circumstances and have<a></a> been\nconsistently applied and adequately disclosed; the reasonableness of\nsignificant<a></a> accounting estimates made by the directors; and\nthe overall presentation of the financial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>In addition, we read all the financial and\nnon-financial information in the<a></a> Annual Report to identify\nmaterial inconsistencies with the audited financial statements and to identify\nany information that is materially incorrect based on, or materially<a></a> inconsistent with, the knowledge acquired by us in the course\nof performing the audit. If<a></a> we become aware of any apparent\nmaterial misstatements or inconsistencies we consider the<a></a>\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span (Revised) the company is exempt from<a></a> the\n requirements to prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a wholly-owned<a></a> subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has prepared a\n consolidated cash flow<a></a> statement.</span></ix:exclude><div style=\"display:none\">true</div></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></div><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Turnover</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Turnover which is stated net of\n VAT comprises amounts charged in respect of the<a></a> provision\n of building services and revenues earned on long term contracts.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Interest\nreceivable and interest payable</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest receivable and payable are\nrecognised in the period in which they fall<a></a> due.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Interest earned on amounts received in\nadvance of future construction work<a></a> is deferred and included\nwithin creditors as a component of payments on account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Dividends</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Dividend distributions to the company's\nshareholders are recognised in the financial statements in the period in which\nthe dividends are paid or approved by the company's shareholders.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Work in progress</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Work in progress includes costs incurred\nunder both construction and development contracts.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Work in progress on construction\ncontracts is stated at the lower of cost and net<a></a> realisable\nvalue.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Cost includes construction costs\nand development expenditure, including employee and related costs.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Development contracts are accounted for\nas long term contracts in accordance with<a></a> SSAP9. Turnover on\nsuch contracts is calculated by reference to the estimated value<a></a>\nof work performed to date as a proportion of the total anticipated cost of the<a></a> project. Profit is recognised when the final outcome of the\nproject can be assessed<a></a> with reasonable certainty, by\nincluding in the profit and loss account turnover<a></a> and\nrelated costs as contract activity progresses.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other\ndebtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors are recognised initially at fair\nvalue.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A provision for impairment is\nestablished where there is objective evidence that the company will not be able\nto collect all amounts due according to the original terms of the debtor\nconcerned.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;&#xD;&#xA;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:&#xD;&#xA;AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection17\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other\ncreditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade and other\ncreditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current tax is provided at amounts\nexpected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates and laws that have been\nenacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet date. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax assets and liabilities\narise from timing differences between the recognition of gains and losses in\nthe financial statements and their recognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under FRS 19 deferred tax is recognised\nin respect of all timing differences that have originated but not reversed at\nthe balance sheet date where transactions or events that result in an\nobligation to pay more tax in the future or a right to pay less tax in the\nfuture have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as recoverable and therefore\nrecognised only when, on the basis of all available evidence, it can be\nregarded as more likely than not that there will be suitable taxable profits\nfrom which the future reversal of the underlying timing differences can be\ndeducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is not recognised when\nfixed assets are revalued unless by the balance sheet date there is a binding\nagreement to sell the revalued assets and the gain or loss expected to arise on\nsale has been recognised in the financial statements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred tax is measured on a discounted\nbasis to reflect the time value of money over the period between the balance\nsheet date and the dates on which it is estimated that the timing differences\nwill reverse, or where the timing differences are not expected to reverse, a\nperiod not exceeding 50 years. <span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> </span>Discount\nrates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been adopted reflecting the post-tax yield to\nmaturity that can be obtained on government bonds with similar maturity dates\nand currencies to those of the deferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Pensions</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>The company operates a defined\ncontribution pension scheme. Pension contributions in respect of this scheme\nare accrued as they fall due.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;&#xD;&#xA;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:&#xD;&#xA;AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection18\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Share based\npayments</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Shares in Songbird Estates plc held by\nthe Canary Wharf Employees' Share Ownership Plan Trust may be allocated to\nemployees of the company under the terms of share schemes or allocations\nadopted from time to time by the company.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The terms of an allocation may, at the option of the company, allow the\nemployee to receive a cash settlement in lieu of their share allocation.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>In this event, the cash amount receivable by\nan employee is calculated by reference to the market price of the shares at\nthat date.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Where the terms of an allocation permit\nthe employee to opt for a cash settlement, the allocation is accounted for as a\ncash settled share based payment.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Where\nthe terms of the allocation allow, but do not require, the company to offer a\ncash settlement option to the employees, the allocation is accounted for as an\nequity settled share based payment.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;&#xD;&#xA;text-indent:-23.2pt;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>For cash settled share allocations, a\nliability is recorded based on the market value of the shares at each balance sheet\ndate.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The cost of equity settled share\nallocations is measured at the grant date based on the market value of the\nshares at that date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The associated cost\nis charged to the same expense category as the employment cost of the relevant\nemployee, spread on a straight line basis over the relevant vesting period,\nbased on the company's estimate of the shares that will eventually vest.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span
